margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;"><span style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; font-weight: 600; box-sizing: border-box;">（3）TypedArray(typedArray)</span></p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">TypedArray数组的构造函数，可以接受另一个TypedArray实例作为参数。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">var typedArray = new Int8Array(new Uint8Array(4));
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">Int8Array</code>构造函数接受一个<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">Uint8Array</code>实例作为参数。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">注意，此时生成的新数组，只是复制了参数数组的值，对应的底层内存是不一样的。新数组会开辟一段新的内存储存数据，不会在原数组的内存之上建立视图。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">var x = new Int8Array([1, 1]);
var y = new Int8Array(x);
x[0] // 1
y[0] // 1

x[0] = 2;
y[0] // 1
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，数组<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">y</code>是以数组<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">x</code>为模板而生成的，当<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">x</code>变动的时候，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">y</code>并没有变动。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">如果想基于同一段内存，构造不同的视图，可以采用下面的写法。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">var x = new Int8Array([1, 1]);
var y = new Int8Array(x.buffer);
x[0] // 1
y[0] // 1

x[0] = 2;
y[0] // 2
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;"><span style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; font-weight: 600; box-sizing: border-box;">（4）TypedArray(arrayLikeObject)</span></p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">构造函数的参数也可以是一个普通数组，然后直接生成TypedArray实例。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">var typedArray = new Uint8Array([1, 2, 3, 4]);
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">注意，这时TypedArray视图会重新开辟内存，不会在原数组的内存上建立视图。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码从一个普通的数组，生成一个8位无符号整数的TypedArray实例。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">TypedArray数组也可以转换回普通数组。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">var normalArray = Array.prototype.slice.call(typedArray);
</code></pre><h3 id="-" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 24px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; font-size: 1.25em; box-sizing: border-box; line-height: 1.25; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">数组方法</h3><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">普通数组的操作方法和属性，对TypedArray数组完全适用。</p><ul style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">注意，TypedArray数组没有<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">concat</code>方法。如果想要合并多个TypedArray数组，可以用下面这个函数。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">function concatenate(resultConstructor, ...arrays) {
  let totalLength = 0;
  for (let arr of arrays) {
    totalLength += arr.length;
  }
  let result = new resultConstructor(totalLength);
  let offset = 0;
  for (let arr of arrays) {
    result.set(arr, offset);
    offset += arr.length;
  }
  return result;
}

concatenate(Uint8Array, Uint8Array.of(1, 2), Uint8Array.of(3, 4))
// Uint8Array [1, 2, 3, 4]
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">另外，TypedArray数组与普通数组一样，部署了Iterator接口，所以可以被遍历。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">let ui8 = Uint8Array.of(0, 1, 2);
for (let byte of ui8) {
  console.log(byte);
}
// 0
// 1
// 2
</code></pre><h3 id="-" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 24px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; font-size: 1.25em; box-sizing: border-box; line-height: 1.25; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">字节序</h3><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">字节序指的是数值在内存中的表示方式。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">var buffer = new ArrayBuffer(16);
var int32View = new Int32Array(buffer);

for (var i = 0; i &lt; int32View.length; i++) {
  int32View[i] = i * 2;
}
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码生成一个16字节的<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">ArrayBuffer</code>对象，然后在它的基础上，建立了一个32位整数的视图。由于每个32位整数占据4个字节，所以一共可以写入4个整数，依次为0，2，4，6。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">如果在这段数据上接着建立一个16位整数的视图，则可以读出完全不一样的结果。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">var int16View = new Int16Array(buffer);

for (var i = 0; i &lt; int16View.length; i++) {
  console.log("Entry " + i + ": " + int16View[i]);
}
// Entry 0: 0
// Entry 1: 0
// Entry 2: 2
// Entry 3: 0
// Entry 4: 4
// Entry 5: 0
// Entry 6: 6
// Entry 7: 0
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">由于每个16位整数占据2个字节，所以整个<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">ArrayBuffer</code>对象现在分成8段。然后，由于x86体系的计算机都采用小端字节序（little endian），相对重要的字节排在后面的内存地址，相对不重要字节排在前面的内存地址，所以就得到了上面的结果。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">比如，一个占据四个字节的16进制数<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">0x12345678</code>，决定其大小的最重要的字节是“12”，最不重要的是“78”。小端字节序将最不重要的字节排在前面，储存顺序就是<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">78563412</code>；大端字节序则完全相反，将最重要的字节排在前面，储存顺序就是<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">12345678</code>。目前，所有个人电脑几乎都是小端字节序，所以TypedArray数组内部也采用小端字节序读写数据，或者更准确的说，按照本机操作系统设定的字节序读写数据。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">这并不意味大端字节序不重要，事实上，很多网络设备和特定的操作系统采用的是大端字节序。这就带来一个严重的问题：如果一段数据是大端字节序，TypedArray数组将无法正确解析，因为它只能处理小端字节序！为了解决这个问题，JavaScript引入<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">DataView</code>对象，可以设定字节序，下文会详细介绍。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">下面是另一个例子。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">// 假定某段buffer包含如下字节 [0x02, 0x01, 0x03, 0x07]
var buffer = new ArrayBuffer(4);
var v1 = new Uint8Array(buffer);
v1[0] = 2;
v1[1] = 1;
v1[2] = 3;
v1[3] = 7;

var uInt16View = new Uint16Array(buffer);

// 计算机采用小端字节序
// 所以头两个字节等于258
if (uInt16View[0] === 258) {
  console.log('OK'); // "OK"
}

// 赋值运算
uInt16View[0] = 255;    // 字节变为[0xFF, 0x00, 0x03, 0x07]
uInt16View[0] = 0xff05; // 字节变为[0x05, 0xFF, 0x03, 0x07]
uInt16View[1] = 0x0210; // 字节变为[0x05, 0xFF, 0x10, 0x02]
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">下面的函数可以用来判断，当前视图是小端字节序，还是大端字节序。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">const BIG_ENDIAN = Symbol('BIG_ENDIAN');
const LITTLE_ENDIAN = Symbol('LITTLE_ENDIAN');

function getPlatformEndianness() {
  let arr32 = Uint32Array.of(0x12345678);
  let arr8 = new Uint8Array(arr32.buffer);
  switch ((arr8[0]*0x1000000) + (arr8[1]*0x10000) + (arr8[2]*0x100) + (arr8[3])) {
    case 0x12345678:
      return BIG_ENDIAN;
    case 0x78563412:
      return LITTLE_ENDIAN;
    default:
      throw new Error('Unknown endianness');
  }
}
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">总之，与普通数组相比，TypedArray数组的最大优点就是可以直接操作内存，不需要数据类型转换，所以速度快得多。</p><h3 id="bytes_per_element-" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 24px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; font-size: 1.25em; box-sizing: border-box; line-height: 1.25; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">BYTES_PER_ELEMENT属性</h3><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">每一种视图的构造函数，都有一个<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">BYTES_PER_ELEMENT</code>属性，表示这种数据类型占据的字节数。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">Int8Array.BYTES_PER_ELEMENT // 1
Uint8Array.BYTES_PER_ELEMENT // 1
Int16Array.BYTES_PER_ELEMENT // 2
Uint16Array.BYTES_PER_ELEMENT // 2
Int32Array.BYTES_PER_ELEMENT // 4
Uint32Array.BYTES_PER_ELEMENT // 4
Float32Array.BYTES_PER_ELEMENT // 4
Float64Array.BYTES_PER_ELEMENT // 8
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">这个属性在TypedArray实例上也能获取，即有<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">TypedArray.prototype.BYTES_PER_ELEMENT</code>。</p><h3 id="arraybuffer-" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 24px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; font-size: 1.25em; box-sizing: border-box; line-height: 1.25; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">ArrayBuffer与字符串的互相转换</h3><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;"><code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">ArrayBuffer</code>转为字符串，或者字符串转为<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">ArrayBuffer</code>，有一个前提，即字符串的编码方法是确定的。假定字符串采用UTF-16编码（JavaScript的内部编码方式），可以自己编写转换函数。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">// ArrayBuffer转为字符串，参数为ArrayBuffer对象
function ab2str(buf) {
  return String.fromCharCode.apply(null, new Uint16Array(buf));
}

// 字符串转为ArrayBuffer对象，参数为字符串
function str2ab(str) {
  var buf = new ArrayBuffer(str.length * 2); // 每个字符占用2个字节
  var bufView = new Uint16Array(buf);
  for (var i = 0, strLen = str.length; i &lt; strLen; i++) {
    bufView[i] = str.charCodeAt(i);
  }
  return buf;
}
</code></pre><h3 id="-" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 24px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; font-size: 1.25em; box-sizing: border-box; line-height: 1.25; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">溢出</h3><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">不同的视图类型，所能容纳的数值范围是确定的。超出这个范围，就会出现溢出。比如，8位视图只能容纳一个8位的二进制值，如果放入一个9位的值，就会溢出。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">TypedArray数组的溢出处理规则，简单来说，就是抛弃溢出的位，然后按照视图类型进行解释。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">var uint8 = new Uint8Array(1);

uint8[0] = 256;
uint8[0] // 0

uint8[0] = -1;
uint8[0] // 255
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">uint8</code>是一个8位视图，而256的二进制形式是一个9位的值<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">100000000</code>，这时就会发生溢出。根据规则，只会保留后8位，即<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">00000000</code>。<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">uint8</code>视图的解释规则是无符号的8位整数，所以<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">00000000</code>就是<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">0</code>。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">负数在计算机内部采用“2的补码”表示，也就是说，将对应的正数值进行否运算，然后加<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">1</code>。比如，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">-1</code>对应的正值是<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">1</code>，进行否运算以后，得到<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">11111110</code>，再加上<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">1</code>就是补码形式<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">11111111</code>。<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">uint8</code>按照无符号的8位整数解释<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">11111111</code>，返回结果就是<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">255</code>。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">一个简单转换规则，可以这样表示。</p><ul style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px 0px 0px 2em; list-style: none; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;"><li style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box;">正向溢出（overflow）：当输入值大于当前数据类型的最大值，结果等于当前数据类型的最小值加上余值，再减去1。</li><li style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0.25em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box;">负向溢出（underflow）：当输入值小于当前数据类型的最小值，结果等于当前数据类型的最大值减去余值，再加上1。</li></ul><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面的“余值”就是模运算的结果，即 JavaScript 里面的<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">%</code>运算符的结果。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">12 % 4 // 0
12 % 5 // 2
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，12除以4是没有余值的，而除以5会得到余值2。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">请看下面的例子。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">var int8 = new Int8Array(1);

int8[0] = 128;
int8[0] // -128

int8[0] = -129;
int8[0] // 127
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面例子中，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">int8</code>是一个带符号的8位整数视图，它的最大值是127，最小值是-128。输入值为<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">128</code>时，相当于正向溢出<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">1</code>，根据“最小值加上余值（128除以127的余值是1），再减去1”的规则，就会返回<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">-128</code>；输入值为<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">-129</code>时，相当于负向溢出<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">1</code>，根据“最大值减去余值（-129除以-128的余值是1），再加上1”的规则，就会返回<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">127</code>。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;"><code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">Uint8ClampedArray</code>视图的溢出规则，与上面的规则不同。它规定，凡是发生正向溢出，该值一律等于当前数据类型的最大值，即255；如果发生负向溢出，该值一律等于当前数据类型的最小值，即0。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">var uint8c = new Uint8ClampedArray(1);

uint8c[0] = 256;
uint8c[0] // 255

uint8c[0] = -1;
uint8c[0] // 0
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面例子中，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">uint8C</code>是一个<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">Uint8ClampedArray</code>视图，正向溢出时都返回255，负向溢出都返回0。</p><h3 id="typedarray-prototype-buffer" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 24px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; font-size: 1.25em; box-sizing: border-box; line-height: 1.25; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">TypedArray.prototype.buffer</h3><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">TypedArray实例的<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">buffer</code>属性，返回整段内存区域对应的<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">ArrayBuffer</code>对象。该属性为只读属性。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">var a = new Float32Array(64);
var b = new Uint8Array(a.buffer);
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码的<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">a</code>视图对象和<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">b</code>视图对象，对应同一个<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">ArrayBuffer</code>对象，即同一段内存。</p><h3 id="typedarray-prototype-bytelength-typedarray-prototype-byteoffset" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 24px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; font-size: 1.25em; box-sizing: border-box; line-height: 1.25; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">TypedArray.prototype.byteLength，TypedArray.prototype.byteOffset</h3><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;"><code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">byteLength</code>属性返回TypedArray数组占据的内存长度，单位为字节。<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">byteOffset</code>属性返回TypedArray数组从底层<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">ArrayBuffer</code>对象的哪个字节开始。这两个属性都是只读属性。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">var b = new ArrayBuffer(8);

var v1 = new Int32Array(b);
var v2 = new Uint8Array(b, 2);
var v3 = new Int16Array(b, 2, 2);

v1.byteLength // 8
v2.byteLength // 6
v3.byteLength // 4

v1.byteOffset // 0
v2.byteOffset // 2
v3.byteOffset // 2
</code></pre><h3 id="typedarray-prototype-length" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 24px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; font-size: 1.25em; box-sizing: border-box; line-height: 1.25; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">TypedArray.prototype.length</h3><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;"><code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">length</code>属性表示TypedArray数组含有多少个成员。注意将<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">byteLength</code>属性和<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">length</code>属性区分，前者是字节长度，后者是成员长度。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">var a = new Int16Array(8);

a.length // 8
a.byteLength // 16
</code></pre><h3 id="typedarray-prototype-set-" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 24px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; font-size: 1.25em; box-sizing: border-box; line-height: 1.25; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">TypedArray.prototype.set()</h3><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">TypedArray数组的<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">set</code>方法用于复制数组（普通数组或TypedArray数组），也就是将一段内容完全复制到另一段内存。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">var a = new Uint8Array(8);
var b = new Uint8Array(8);

b.set(a);
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码复制<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">a</code>数组的内容到<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">b</code>数组，它是整段内存的复制，比一个个拷贝成员的那种复制快得多。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;"><code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">set</code>方法还可以接受第二个参数，表示从<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">b</code>对象的哪一个成员开始复制<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">a</code>对象。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">var a = new Uint16Array(8);
var b = new Uint16Array(10);

b.set(a, 2)
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码的<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">b</code>数组比<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">a</code>数组多两个成员，所以从<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">b[2]</code>开始复制。</p><h3 id="typedarray-prototype-subarray-" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 24px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; font-size: 1.25em; box-sizing: border-box; line-height: 1.25; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">TypedArray.prototype.subarray()</h3><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;"><code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">subarray</code>方法是对于TypedArray数组的一部分，再建立一个新的视图。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">var a = new Uint16Array(8);
var b = a.subarray(2,3);

a.byteLength // 16
b.byteLength // 2
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;"><code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">subarray</code>方法的第一个参数是起始的成员序号，第二个参数是结束的成员序号（不含该成员），如果省略则包含剩余的全部成员。所以，上面代码的<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">a.subarray(2,3)</code>，意味着b只包含<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">a[2]</code>一个成员，字节长度为2。</p><h3 id="typedarray-prototype-slice-" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 24px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; font-size: 1.25em; box-sizing: border-box; line-height: 1.25; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">TypedArray.prototype.slice()</h3><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">TypeArray实例的<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">slice</code>方法，可以返回一个指定位置的新的TypedArray实例。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">let ui8 = Uint8Array.of(0, 1, 2);
ui8.slice(-1)
// Uint8Array [ 2 ]
</code></pre><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">上面代码中，<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">ui8</code>是8位无符号整数数组视图的一个实例。它的<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">slice</code>方法可以从当前视图之中，返回一个新的视图实例。</p><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;"><code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">slice</code>方法的参数，表示原数组的具体位置，开始生成新数组。负值表示逆向的位置，即-1为倒数第一个位置，-2表示倒数第二个位置，以此类推。</p><h3 id="typedarray-of-" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 24px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; font-size: 1.25em; box-sizing: border-box; line-height: 1.25; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">TypedArray.of()</h3><p style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;;">TypedArray数组的所有构造函数，都有一个静态方法<code style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0.2em 0px; margin: 0px; font-size: 12px; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">of</code>，用于将参数转为一个TypedArray实例。</p><pre style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 16px; padding: 16px; box-sizing: border-box; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.45; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; word-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; background-color: rgb(247, 247, 247); border-radius: 3px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51);"><code class="lang-javascript" style="text-rendering: optimizeLegibility; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; box-sizing: border-box; font-family: Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, Menlo, Courier, monospace; padding: 0px; margin: 0px; background: 0px 0px transparent; border-radius: 3px; word-break: normal; white-space: pre; border: 0px; display: inline; overflow: visible; line-height: inherit; word-wrap: normal; color: rgb(255, 102, 102);">Float32Array.of(0.151, -8, 3.7)
// Float32Array [ 0.151, -8, 3.7 ]
